NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE OF DISSOLUTION OF PARTNERSHIP FIRM
Notice is hereby given under the provision of Section 45 of the Indian Partnership Act, 1932 that the partnership
subsisting between us carrying on business in partnership at “Viyasar Illam”, 33, Navabath Kana Street, Madurai-625 001
under the name and style of “Dhanalakshmi Industries” registered on 30-05-1994 bearing No.149/1994 was dissolved
on 14-10-2014 by mutual consent.
Madurai-625 001,
24th November 2014.

for Dhanalakshmi Industries
T.V.K. SURESHBABU
Partner.

I, M. Arunachalam, son of Nelliyan alias Muthukaruppan and Ponnalagammai, Hindu and born on 26-5-1968 and now
residing at 4/708, Thazhi Veethi, Nehru Street, Anbu Nagar, Madurai-20, having taken in adoption by the adopted parents
(late) Kannappa Chettiar and Meenakshi Achi by a registered deed Document Number 14, dated 09-09-1992, shall
henceforth be known as KN. VEERAPPAN.
Madurai,
28th November 2014.

Yours faithfully,
M. ARUNACHALAM.

M. Jothiprakash a Male Child born to M. Murugesan, on 10th July 1992, residing at No. 97A, Kamarajar Colony
8th Street, Kodambakkam, Chennai-600 024, has been living as a Female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
by Dr. V. Jayaraman, (Regn: 32070) Professor of Plastic Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College of Head of upgraded
Burns unit, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010. By This I May be treated as a Female and henceforth
be known as M. PRAGALYA.
Chennai, 600 024,
28th November 2014.

M. JOTHIPRAKASH.
